733<div class="css-6n7j50">

734<button aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Account" class="e1j3jvdr4 css-114fczm" data-testid="user-settings-button" type="button">

738<circle cx="8" cy="4" r="4">

740</svg>

746</div>

749<div class="css-1sojcmr ehdk2mb0">

750<h1 id="link-24b0de36" class="css-1o6zoyt e1h9rw200" data-testid="headline">

751Why Is CBD Everywhere?</h1>

752</div>

753<p class="css-1b6a17a e1wiw3jv0">

754Cannabidiol is being touted as a magical elixir, a cure-all now available in bath bombs, dog treats and even pharmaceuticals. But maybe it’s just a fix for our anxious times.</p>

755</div>

756</div>

757</header>

758<div class="css-yi0xdk e89cr9k0">

855Alex Williams</span>

859<ul class="css-1u1psjv epjyd6m3">

860<li class="css-ccw2r3 epjyd6m2">

862Oct. 27, 2018</time>

866</div>

867</div>

868<section name="articleBody" class="meteredContent css-1r7ky0e">

869<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

870<div class="css-53u6y8">

871<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

872It’s hard to say the precise moment when CBD, the voguish cannabis derivative, went from being a fidget spinner alternative for stoners to a mainstream panacea.</p>

873<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

874Maybe it was in January, when Mandy Moore, hours before the Golden Globes, <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="http://coveteur.com/2018/01/09/mandy-moore-use-cbd-oil-feet-heel-pain/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

875told Coveteur</a>

876 that she was experimenting with CBD oil to relieve the pain from wearing high heels. “It could be a really exciting evening,” she said. “I could be floating this year.”</p>

877<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

878Maybe it was in July, when Willie Nelson introduced a line of CBD-infused coffee beans called <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="http://tasteofcountry.com/willie-nelson-willies-remedy-cbd-oil-cannabis-products/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

879Willie’s Remedy</a>

880. “It’s two of my favorites, together in the perfect combination,” he said in a statement.</p>

881</div>

882<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

883</aside>

884</div>

885<div class="">

886</div>

887<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

888<div class="css-53u6y8">

889<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

890Or maybe it was earlier this month, when Dr. Sanjay Gupta gave a qualified endorsement of CBD on <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=nTB3HGJOYt4" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

891“The Dr. Oz Show.”</a>

892 “I think there is a legitimate medicine here,” he said. “We’re talking about something that could really help people.”</p>

893</div>

894<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

895</aside>

896</div>

897<div class="">

898<div>

899</div>

900</div>

901<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

902<div class="css-53u6y8">

903<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

904So the question now becomes: Is this the dawning of a new miracle elixir, or does all the hype mean we have already reached Peak CBD?</p>

905<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

906Either way, it would be hard to script a more of-the-moment salve for a nation on edge. With its proponents claiming that CBD treats ailments as diverse as inflammation, pain, acne, anxiety, insomnia, depression, post-traumatic stress and even cancer, it’s easy to wonder if this all natural, non-psychotropic and widely available cousin of marijuana represents a cure for the 21st century itself.</p>

907<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

908The ice caps are melting, the Dow teeters, and a divided country seems headed for divorce court. Is it any wonder, then, that everyone seems to be reaching for the tincture?</p>

909<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

910“Right now, CBD is the chemical equivalent to Bitcoin in 2016,” said Jason DeLand, a New York advertising executive and a board member of <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://dosist.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

911Dosist</a>

912, a cannabis company in <!-- -->

913Santa Monica, Calif<!-- -->

914., that makes disposable vape pens with CBD. “It’s hot, everywhere and yet almost nobody understands it.”</p>

915</div>

916<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

917</aside>

918</div>

919<div class="">

920</div>

921<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

922<div class="css-53u6y8">

923<h2 class="css-ow6j0y eoo0vm40" id="link-a36fb6a">

924Cannabis for Non-Stoners</h2>

925<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

926With CBD popping up in nearly everything — bath bombs, ice cream, dog treats — it is hard to overstate the speed at which CBD has moved from the Burning Man margins to the cultural center. </p>

927<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

928A year ago, it was easy to be blissfully unaware of CBD. Now, to measure the hype, it’s as if everyone suddenly discovered yoga. Or penicillin. Or maybe oxygen.</p>

929<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

930Even so, you ask, what <em class="css-2fg4z9 e1gzwzxm0">

931is</em>

932 CBD? Plenty of people still have no idea. CBD is short for cannabidiol, an abundant chemical in the cannabis plant. Unlike its more famous cannabinoid cousin, THC (tetrahydrocannabinol), CBD does not make you stoned.</p>

933<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

934Which is not to say that you feel utterly normal when you take it. </p>

935</div>

936<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

937</aside>

938</div>

939<div class="">

940<div class="css-79elbk" data-testid="photoviewer-wrapper">

941<div class="css-z3e15g" data-testid="photoviewer-wrapper-hidden">

942</div>

943<div data-testid="photoviewer-children" class="css-1a48zt4 e11si9ry5">

944<figure class="img-sz-medium css-1l3p632 e1g7ppur0" aria-label="media" role="group">

945<div class="css-1xdhyk6 erfvjey0">

946<span class="css-1ly73wi e1tej78p0">

947Image</span>

948<img alt="CBD drops by a New York start-up called Plant People. The product purports to relieve stress, reduce pain and improve cognition. " class="css-r3fift" src="https://static01.nyt.com/images/2018/10/28/fashion/28CBD7/merlin_145837626_3002f994-325f-4db0-b8bf-c7e22cff9f7a-articleLarge.jpg?quality=75&amp;auto=webp&amp;disable=upscale" srcSet="https://static01.nyt.com/images/2018/10/28/fashion/28CBD7/merlin_145837626_3002f994-325f-4db0-b8bf-c7e22cff9f7a-articleLarge.jpg?quality=75&amp;auto=webp 600w,https://static01.nyt.com/images/2018/10/28/fashion/28CBD7/merlin_145837626_3002f994-325f-4db0-b8bf-c7e22cff9f7a-jumbo.jpg?quality=75&amp;auto=webp 1024w,https://static01.nyt.com/images/2018/10/28/fashion/28CBD7/merlin_145837626_3002f994-325f-4db0-b8bf-c7e22cff9f7a-superJumbo.jpg?quality=75&amp;auto=webp 2048w" sizes="((min-width: 600px) and (max-width: 1004px)) 84vw, (min-width: 1005px) 60vw, 100vw" decoding="async" width="600" height="400"/>

949</div>

950<figcaption class="css-1l44abu ewdxa0s0">

951<span aria-hidden="true" class="css-16f3y1r e13ogyst0">

952CBD drops by a New York start-up called Plant People. The product purports to relieve stress, reduce pain and improve cognition. </span>

953<span class="css-cnj6d5 e1z0qqy90">

954<span class="css-1ly73wi e1tej78p0">

955Credit...</span>

956<span>

957Jules Davies</span>

958</span>

959</figcaption>

960</figure>

961</div>

962</div>

963</div>

964<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

965<div class="css-53u6y8">

966<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

967Users speak of a “body” high, as opposed to a mind-altering one. “Physically, it’s like taking a warm bath, melting the tension away,” said Gabe Kennedy, 27, a founder of <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://plantpeople.co/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

968Plant People</a>

969, a start-up in New York that sells CBD capsules and oils. “It is balancing; a leveling, smoothing sensation in the body mostly, and an evenness of attention in the mind.”</p>

970</div>

971<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

972</aside>

973</div>

974<div class="">

975<div>

976</div>

977</div>

978<div class="">

979</div>

980<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

981<div class="css-53u6y8">

982<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

983Comparing it to the feeling after an intense meditation or yoga session, Mr. Kennedy added that the CBD glow has “synergistic downstream effects” in terms of social connections. “Around others, I find myself more present and attentive, more creative and open.”</p>

984<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

985Moreover, you are unlikely to find yourself <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://medium.com/@cbdprofessor/will-cbd-oil-give-me-the-munchies-96ad61319ea6" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

986microwaving frozen burritos</a>

987 at midnight after taking CBD, unlike with pot.</p>

988<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

989Such quasi-religious talk is common among CBD’s disciples.</p>

990<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

991“I’m a 30 y.o. male who has not experienced a single anxiety free day in my adult life,” wrote one user on a <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.reddit.com/r/CBD/comments/9muel3/it_changed_my_life/?utm_content=title&amp;utm_medium=hot&amp;utm_source=reddit&amp;utm_name=CBD" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

992CBD forum on Reddit</a>

993 earlier this month. “About 3 weeks ago I started taking CBD-oil 10 percent and I can’t even describe how amazing I feel. For the first time in 15+ years I feel happy and look forward to living a long life.”</p>

994<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

995Such testimonials make CBD seem like a perfect cure for our times. Every cultural era, after all, has its defining psychological malady. This also means that every era has its signature drug.</p>

996<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

997The jittery postwar era, with its backyard bomb shelters and suburban fears about keeping up with the Joneses, gave rise to a boom in sedatives, as seen in the era’s pop songs (<a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://io9.gizmodo.com/this-is-the-drug-in-the-rolling-stones-song-mothers-li-1693032181" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

998“Mother’s Little Helper,”</a>

999 by the Rolling Stones) and best sellers (“Valley of the Dolls,” by Jacqueline Susann).</p>

1000<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1001The recessionary 1990s gave rise to Generation X angst, Kurt Cobain dirges and a cultural obsession with newfangled antidepressants (see Elizabeth Wurtzel’s “<a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.nytimes.com/1994/09/25/books/rambunctious-with-tears.html?module=inline" title="">

1002Prozac Nation: Young and Depressed in America</a>

1003”).</p>

1004</div>

1005<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1006</aside>

1007</div>

1008<div class="">

1009</div>

1010<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1011<div class="css-53u6y8">

1012<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1013The defining sociological condition today, especially among millennials, is arguably <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2017/06/10/style/anxiety-is-the-new-depression-xanax.html" title="">

1014anxiety</a>

1015: anxiety about our political dysfunction, anxiety about terrorism, anxiety about climate change, anxiety about student loan debt, even anxiety about <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2017/12/11/style/robots-jobs-children.html" title="">

1016artificial intelligence taking away </a>

1017all the good jobs.</p>

1018<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1019The anxiety feels even more acute since the wired generation feels continuously bombarded by new reasons to freak out, thanks to their smart devices.</p>

1020<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1021“You are inundated with terrible news, and you have no choice to opt in or out,” said Verena von Pfetten, 35, the former digital director for Lucky magazine who is a founder of <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.gossamer.co/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1022Gossamer</a>

1023, a high-style magazine targeted to cannabis-loving tastemakers. “You open your computer, check your phone, there are news alerts.”</p>

1024<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1025What a convenient time for Mother Nature to bestow a perma-chillax cure that seems to tie together so many cultural threads at once: our obsession with self-care and wellness, the mainstreaming of alternative therapies and the relentless march of legalized marijuana.</p>

1026<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1027“That seems like a gift in these times,” Ms. von Pfetten said.</p>

1028</div>

1029<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1030</aside>

1031</div>

1038<div class="css-1xdhyk6 erfvjey0">

1058<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1059<div class="css-53u6y8">

1060<h2 class="css-ow6j0y eoo0vm40" id="link-c765c39">

1061‘The New Avocado Toast’</h2>

1062<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1063The tsunami of CBD-infused products has hit so suddenly, and with such force, that marketers have strained to find a fitting analogy. Chris Burggraeve, a former Coca-Cola and Ab InBev executive, called it the <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.businessinsider.com/cbd-and-cannabis-create-food-industry-buzz-2018-10" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1064“new avocado toast,</a>

1065”<!-- -->

1066 in an interview with Business Insider. </p>

1067</div>

1068<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1069</aside>

1070</div>

1071<div class="">

1072</div>

1073<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1074<div class="css-53u6y8">

1075<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1076Then again, avocado toast seems so five years ago. </p>

1077<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1078Fad chasers looking for the next<em class="css-2fg4z9 e1gzwzxm0">

1079-</em>

1080next big thing may want to check out the <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://guestofaguest.com/new-york/food/cbd-toast-is-nycs-chillest-brunch-must-have" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1081CBD-infused ricotta-and-honey toast</a>

1082 at <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://chillhouse.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1083Chillhouse</a>

1084, the Instagram-ready coffee shop, nail salon and massage studio on the Lower East Side of Manhattan. And then retreat to <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2018/01/04/nyregion/want-a-better-workout-just-breathe.html" title="">

1085Inscape NYC</a>

1086, a meditation and relaxation studio in Chelsea, to unwind with a stress-busting <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.inscape.life/events/2018/9/19/cbd-saturdays" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1087CBD Saturday</a>

1088 session.</p>

1089<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1090It would be false to suggest CBD is nothing more than an obsession for reiki-adjacent bicoastal millennials. According to the <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.aarp.org/health/conditions-treatments/info-2018/cbd-oil-marijuana-health-benefits.html" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1091AARP website</a>

1092, CBD has become a popular treatment for pain and arthritis among baby boomers, some of whom may have been out of the cannabis game since they rolled their last doobie at a Foghat concert in <!-- -->

10931975<!-- -->

1094.</p>

1095<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1096Even so, CBD seems to have found its natural target audience among the vegan-curious creative professionals who cluster in trendy hotels like the James New York-Nomad hotel, which offers a <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.jameshotels.com/new-york/nomad/restaurant-bar/in-room-dining/cbd-menu" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1097room-service CBD tasting menu</a>

1098 featuring CBD-infused meatballs and sriracha-mayo House Tots. Or the Standard hotel outposts in Miami and New York, which sell $50 blood orange-flavored gumdrops by the upscale CBD brand <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.lordjones.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1099Lord Jones</a>

1100 in its minibars.</p>

1101</div>

1102<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1103</aside>

1104</div>

1105<div class="">

1106<div class="css-79elbk" data-testid="photoviewer-wrapper">

1107<div class="css-z3e15g" data-testid="photoviewer-wrapper-hidden">

1108</div>

1109<div data-testid="photoviewer-children" class="css-1a48zt4 e11si9ry5">

1110<figure class="img-sz-medium css-1l3p632 e1g7ppur0" aria-label="media" role="group">

1111<div class="css-1xdhyk6 erfvjey0">

1112<span class="css-1ly73wi e1tej78p0">

1113Image</span>

1114<div class="css-zjzyr8" data-testid="lazy-image">

1115<div data-testid="lazyimage-container" style="height:350.5777777777777px">

1116</div>

1117</div>

1118</div>

1119<figcaption class="css-1l44abu ewdxa0s0">

1120<span aria-hidden="true" class="css-16f3y1r e13ogyst0">

1121Blood orange and CBD-infused gumdrops by an upscale brand called Lord Jones, which is sold at trendy hotels.</span>

1122</figcaption>

1123</figure>

1124</div>

1125</div>

1126</div>

1127<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1128<div class="css-53u6y8">

1129<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1130Such sumptuously packaged, premium-priced CBD products appeal to trend-conscious consumers in part because they promise a degree of indulgence — without the indulgence.</p>

1131<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1132Despite its cannabis origins, CBD is not marketed as a recreational drug, but almost as its opposite: as a corrective to the ill effects of alcohol and even marijuana itself, which makes it catnip for hard-charging professionals who need to be fresh for a 7 a.m. breakfast meeting. </p>

1133</div>

1134<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1135</aside>

1136</div>

1137<div class="">

1138</div>

1139<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1140<div class="css-53u6y8">

1141<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1142A detox drink under development called <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.indiegogo.com/projects/sober-up-detox-shot" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1143Sober Up</a>

1144, for example, will contain CBD and is supposed to support liver health and help prevent hangovers.</p>

1145<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1146Fewer hangovers is also the sales pitch at <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.adriaenblocknyc.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1147Adriaen Block</a>

1148, a bar in the Astoria neighborhood of Queens that whips up CBD-infused negronis and old-fashioned cocktails. “You can maintain a conversation and know what you are saying,” said Zsolt Csonka, who owns the bar and mixes drinks there. “After two or three drinks, you’ll be able to go to the gym the next day.</p>

1149<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1150When added to dishes like sesame shrimp toast at <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.popcultivate.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1151PopCultivate</a>

1152, a series of cannabis-centric pop-up dinners in Los Angeles, CBD (which is flavorless) can function as a social lubricant, just like a wine pairing, but without, according to proponents, the hangover.</p>

1153<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1154“You become more engaged with your neighbors, talk more freely, and meet more people you dine with,” said Chris Yang, the molecular biologist turned chef behind the series.</p>

1155<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1156But nowhere does the fervor for CBD seem greater than in health and beauty, where cannabidiol is often packaged with buzzy terms like “single origin,” “small batch” and “plant based.”</p>

1157<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1158Among beauty products alone, CBD has already <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2018/01/30/style/cbd-oil-beauty-cannabis-pain-relief.html" title="">

1159achieved cliché status</a>

1160, popping up in <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.myaderm.com/products/myaderm-cbd-blemish-cream?variant=8108459982958" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1161blemish creams</a>

1162, <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://kanaskincare.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1163sleeping masks</a>

1164, <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://cbddailyproducts.com/product/cbd-shampoo/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1165shampoo</a>

1166s, hair conditioners, <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.cbdforlife.us/products/cbd-eye-serum/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1167eye serums</a>

1168, anti-acne lotions, mascaras, massage oils, soaps, lip balms, bath bombs, anti-wrinkle serums, muscle rubs and a Sephora aisle’s worth of moisturizers, face lotions and body creams. Even the bedroom is not safe from the CBD invasion, to judge by the spate of CBD <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://privypeach.com/products/cbd-infused-personal-lubricant" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1169sexual lubricants</a>

1170 on shelves.</p>

1171</div>

1172<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1173</aside>

1174</div>

1175<div class="">

1176</div>

1177<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1178<div class="css-53u6y8">

1179<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1180“<a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.glamour.com/gallery/cbd-beauty-products?verso=true" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1181I replaced my entire beauty routine with only CBD products</a>

1182,” read a recent headline in Glamour magazine. </p>

1183<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1184This earthy, artisanal aura plays well with devotees of, say, Goop, who are already conditioned, after years of aromatherapy, cryotherapy and homeopathy, to accept a natural wellness mantra over anything on offer by Big Pharma and the medical industrial complex.</p>

1185<div>

1186</div>

1187<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1188As an alternative health regimen, CBD holds particular appeal to women, said Gretchen Lidicker, the health editor of <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.mindbodygreen.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1189Mindbodygreen</a>

1190, a wellness website based in New York, and the author of <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="http://www.countrymanpress.com/category/upcoming/book/5a8f75a2e516eb13044164ab" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1191“CBD Oil Everyday Secrets.”</a>

1192 Noting the preponderance of female-run CBD businesses, Ms. Lidicker, 26, said that it is “no surprise that women are leading the CBD movement.”</p>

1193<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1194“Women have long felt ignored and dehumanized by the medical and health care industries,” she said. “They experience longer wait times for treatment. Their pain and suffering are more likely to be dismissed as anxiety or hysteria. And the male body has typically been the model for medical research.” </p>

1195<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1196Such concerns seem to have helped fuel the CBD movement. In an era marked by a loss of faith traditional institutions (governments, banks, hospitals), CBD has flourished, perhaps because it seems new, mysterious and untainted by the mainstream. </p>

1197<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1198It may or may not be a coincidence that one of the best-known CBD retailers in New York, <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.thealchemistskitchen.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1199the Alchemist’s Kitchen</a>

1200 in the East Village, serves up cannabidiol tinctures and gel caps, alongside workshops on astrocartography, lucid dreaming and full-moon ancestral healing.</p>

1201</div>

1202<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1203</aside>

1204</div>

1205<div class="">

1206</div>

1207<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1208<div class="css-53u6y8">

1209<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1210And devotees swear it works. “It really helps with pain, inflammation and the general anxiety that grips me 24 hour a day,” said Anna Duckworth, 34, the editor of <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.missgrass.com/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1211Miss Grass</a>

1212, a website based in Venice, Calif., that W magazine called the <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.wmagazine.com/story/miss-grass-goop-cannabis" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1213“Goop of cannabis.”</a>

1214 </p>

1215<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1216“There are millions and millions of people who are just fed up and don’t want to take these drugs that make them feel bad,” she said, “and want to go a more nontoxic, natural route.”</p>

1217</div>

1218<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1219</aside>

1220</div>

1221<div class="">

1222<div class="css-79elbk" data-testid="photoviewer-wrapper">

1223<div class="css-z3e15g" data-testid="photoviewer-wrapper-hidden">

1225<div data-testid="photoviewer-children" class="css-1a48zt4 e11si9ry5">

1226<figure class="img-sz-large css-1viisko e1g7ppur0" aria-label="media" role="group">

1227<div class="css-1xdhyk6 erfvjey0">

1235<figcaption class="css-18crmh6 ewdxa0s0">

1238Credit...</span>

1241</span>

1242</figcaption>

1244</div>

1247<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1248<div class="css-53u6y8">

1249<h2 class="css-ow6j0y eoo0vm40" id="link-449814e3">

1250Snake Oil or Wonder Drug?</h2>

1251<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1252There’s one problem with that approach. When people turn to CBD-infused coconut lattes to cure acne and erectile dysfunction, it is not easy to separate hype from science.</p>

1253<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1254Skeptics who assume CBD is just 21st-century snake oil, however, may be surprised to learn that the substance is being studied as a potential treatment for maladies as diverse as schizophrenia, insomnia and cancer.</p>

1255<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1256“CBD is the most promising drug that has come out for neuropsychiatric diseases in the last 50 years,” said <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://med.nyu.edu/faculty/esther-blessing" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1257Dr. Esther Blessing</a>

1258, an assistant professor at New York University School of Medicine, who is coordinating a study of CBD as a <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://clinicaltrials.gov/ct2/show/NCT03248167?term=Cannabidiol&amp;cond=PTSD&amp;rank=2" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1259treatment for post-traumatic stress disorder and alcohol use disorder</a>

1260. “The reason it is so promising is that it has a unique combination of safety and effectiveness across of very broad range of conditions.”</p>

1261</div>

1262<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1263</aside>

1264</div>

1265<div class="">

1266</div>

1267<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1268<div class="css-53u6y8">

1269<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1270The National Institutes of Health <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://clinicaltrials.gov/ct2/results?cond=&amp;term=CBD&amp;cntry=&amp;state=&amp;city=&amp;dist=" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1271database</a>

1272 lists about 150 of studies involving CBD as a <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.medicalnewstoday.com/articles/317221.php" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1273treatment for conditions as varied as infantile spasms and Parkinson’s disease</a>

1274.</p>

1275<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1276And the research has led to medical treatments. In June, the Food and Drug Administration approved a cannabidiol-based drug called <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.fda.gov/NewsEvents/Newsroom/PressAnnouncements/ucm611046.htm" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1277Epidiolex</a>

1278 as a treatment for severe forms of epilepsy, representing the first government-sanctioned medical use for CBD.</p>

1279<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1280Preliminary research also indicates that CBD may be effective as an antipsychotic in reducing the <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pubmed/22832859" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1281symptoms of schizophrenia</a>

1282, with fewer side effects compared with current antipsychotic drugs, Dr. Blessing said.</p>

1283</div>

1284<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1285</aside>

1286</div>

1287<div class="">

1288<div class="css-79elbk" data-testid="photoviewer-wrapper">

1289<div class="css-z3e15g" data-testid="photoviewer-wrapper-hidden">

1290</div>

1291<div data-testid="photoviewer-children" class="css-1a48zt4 e11si9ry5">

1292<figure class="img-sz-medium css-3mi1lt e1g7ppur0" aria-label="media" role="group">

1293<div class="css-1xdhyk6 erfvjey0">

1294<span class="css-1ly73wi e1tej78p0">

1295Image</span>

1296<div class="css-zjzyr8" data-testid="lazy-image">

1297<div data-testid="lazyimage-container" style="height:552.9333333333333px">

1298</div>

1299</div>

1300</div>

1301<figcaption class="css-1l44abu ewdxa0s0">

1302<span aria-hidden="true" class="css-16f3y1r e13ogyst0">

1303A disposable CBD vape pen by Dosist, a cannabis company in Santa Monica, Calif.</span>

1304</figcaption>

1305</figure>

1306</div>

1307</div>

1308</div>

1309<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1310<div class="css-53u6y8">

1311<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1312CBD has also shown promise to <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC4604178/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1313reduce cravings among people addicted to opioids</a>

1314, according to a study published in Neurotherapeutics in 2015. It may fight cancer, too. The authors of a <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/pmc/articles/PMC3579246/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1315review</a>

1316 published in the British Journal of Clinical Pharmacology in 2012 wrote: “evidence is emerging to suggest that CBD is a potent inhibitor of both cancer growth and spread.”</p>

1317<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1318That’s not to say that a CBD-laced gummy or two should be considered medicine.</p>

1319<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1320“Most of the products where people are putting CBD in coffee or food, there’s no solid evidence that they contain enough CBD to do anything,” Dr. Blessing said. “A CBD coffee may only have five milligrams in it. In order to treat anxiety, we know you need around 300 milligrams.”</p>

1321</div>

1322<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1323</aside>

1324</div>

1325<div class="">

1326</div>

1327<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1328<div class="css-53u6y8">

1329<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1330Don’t go chugging a shot of CBD oil just yet, though. Dr. Blessing said that much of the research is in its infancy, and the purity and dosage of some CBD consumer products may not reliable. And, she noted, CBD can have negative interactions with many medications, so potential users should talk to their doctors before taking it.”</p>

1331<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1332There are legal hazards as well. As with all cannabis products, the federal government categorizes <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.wthr.com/article/new-cbd-oil-drug-first-us-recognized-legal-under-federal-law" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1333CBD products other than Epidiolex</a>

1334 as a Schedule 1 drug, like heroin, according to the Drug Enforcement Administration. And cannabis remains illegal under federal law, even in states that have legalized marijuana for medical or recreational use.</p>

1335<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1336Even so, the D.E.A.’s mission is to go after large-scale drug traffickers, not individual users, said Barbara Carreno, an agency spokeswoman. “We’re not swatting joints out of hands in Hilo, Hawaii, and we’re not going to focus on somebody who is buying lotion or ice cream that has CBD in it.”</p>

1337<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1338Although there have been scattered raids of CBD retailers around the country, several states, including Alabama, Texas, Florida and Oklahoma, have passed laws approving specific CBD products to treat specific ailments. And CBD shops have cropped up nationwide, in Los Angeles, Oklahoma City and <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="http://austin.culturemap.com/news/city-life/04-24-18-hemp-marijuana-cbd-oil-shop-rawsome-rosewood-avenue-east-austin/" title="" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

1339Austin</a>

1340, Tex., to name just a few cities.</p>

1341<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1342In New York City, for example, CBD tinctures and other products can be bought at specialty shops, health food stores, yoga studios, flea markets, boutiques and even some corner delis. (The availability of CBD is perhaps not surprising, given Mayor Bill de Blasio’s continued efforts to reduce the penalties for low-level <a class="css-1g7m0tk" href="https://www.nytimes.com/2018/06/19/nyregion/nypd-marijuana-arrests-new-york-city.html" title="">

1343marijuana violations</a>

1344.)</p>

1345<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1346Aside from a federal crackdown, the only thing that may eventually kill CBD’s momentum is hype itself, said Mr. DeLand of Dosist.</p>

1347</div>

1348<aside class="css-ew4tgv" aria-label="companion column">

1349</aside>

1350</div>

1351<div class="">

1352</div>

1353<div class="css-s99gbd StoryBodyCompanionColumn">

1354<div class="css-53u6y8">

1355<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1356The frothy claims about CBD “sets up some false expectations that the molecule will never be able to live up to,” Mr. DeLand said. Not only are questionable claims an invitation for government regulation, but they risk making even legitimate applications seem dubious, he said. </p>

1357<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1358“In isolation, CBD obviously does have some benefits, but it’s certainly not a catchall for all the world’s health problems,” he said. “We are at the tip of the iceberg on what its therapeutic applications are, and how to make those applications repeatable.”</p>

1359<p class="css-axufdj evys1bk0">

1360“The future of this industry,” Mr. DeLand added, “is going to be based on fact, not fiction.”</p>

1361</div>

1363</aside>
